<text>Where do I even begin?
I will start off by saying that I do not know how TM Noodle is still in business.
Our food did not taste authentic by any means at all. It was so bad that both the Curry and the Lemongrass Beef dish's gravy, looked grey and tasted like it was made from a gravy powder packet.
The rice did not taste fresh. In fact, if I didn't know any better, I would say the rice was cooked several days prior to my visit, and then microwaved. Their Pho was mediocre. I was told AFTER my Pho was presented to me, that there was no lime. For me, lime is a key component to a great tasting Pho soup. All of the items I ordered, the portion sizes were SMALL. If you ever had spring rolls from any other restaurant, imagine being served half of the size of the one you've eaten before. Every item on the menu was overpriced.
No drinks listed on the menu. Once our drinks were brought to us, we were never asked again if we wanted a refill.
If I had to say anything positive at all about this place, it would be that the lady seemed nice, despite her checking on us to see if we needed refills. I consider myself to be pretty easy going. I never complain and I am never that person to knit pick my food. Sadly, this takes the cake. This is the WORST restaurant food I have ever had in my life!

<date>1496023003873</date>< Rating>

< Review>
I have been eating here since Los Amigos opened. The quality has steadily slipped over the last few months. We've provided feedback to the staff and no one seems genuine about what we have to say. Today was the last and final time we will ever eat at Los Amigos. Every single item ordered did not match the ingredients listed on the menu. I asked for extra sides of sour cream and green sauce, was charged for them, and then never received them. The "burritos" were nothing more than canned re fried beans drowning in sauce with a tortilla somewhere in the mix. Unappetizing to look at and even worse to try to eat. When I called to politely inquire about the missing sides and awful burritos, I was argumentatively told that they were "busy" and were unable to do anything about the inedible food. Roughly $40 dollars, zero customer service, and general apathy towards legitimate concerns means I can not recommend Los Amigos nor will I eat there ever again. I will also not patron the owner's other restaurants and establishments in the community including Fratelli's Pizzeria due to the shameful lack of customer service. I wish this was the one and only time experiencing this that prompted me to post this review, however, this was the final straw. Two stars only because your food and customer service used to be something my family and I looked forward to.<//Review>

<Review>I used to work for the Koehls in 1987  when they were just getting started. I knew them to be the kindest most compassionate loving family and friend to their employees. Hard working and completely dedicated to their craft. I  remember them making me feel part of the family  and special

< text>
Although I have never been here in person, I love this company. Here is a Shoutout to Skullduggery:

A few months ago back in June 2020, I bought an An African Elephant motorized 3D puzzle and put it together. However one of the puzzle pieces broke. So I e-mailed the manufacturer and asked for a replacement piece of the one that broke. Not only did Peter Koehl respond to the e-mail and say he would send me another replacement piece, but the company also blessed me with another African Elephant 3D motorized puzzle and surprised me with a B-29 Bomber 3d motorized puzzle. It got shipped to my house and I did not have to pay for anything, not even shipping.

This company goes above and beyond serving its customers. Their customer service exceeds beyond what most companies do today.
I am very thankful and happy that this company cares for its customers and was able to fufill my request.
Skullduggery transforms something that is disapointing to something even better than before.</text>

<Review>This Tacos Mexico in particular is the best one. Been coming here since 1993, and like it as much now as I did the first time I decided to give it a shot. The food is delicious, the staff is very clean, and super friendly. My personal favorite is the BUCHE burrito Ortega the CARNITAS taco. Both with the red sauce. Make sure to request the salsa on the side, since it's a bit spicy. The music that auto plays from the juke box is a bit loud, but goes well with the atmosphere as well as the soccer channel on both TV's. It's a very small restaurant with indoor/outdoor seating.
